 Donors of Ashta Siddhi Nine Funds
 
 
 as bar dinh janaki mata
 
 
 
 hanuman chalisa kii ye chaoupaaiyaan to aapane suni hi hongi lekin kya aapako inkaa sahi arth maaloom hai?kya he siddhiyon or nidhiyon kaa mahatvashriram bhakt hanuman ko aath siddhiyon or nau nidhiyon kaa vardaan maa janaki ne diya tha or kehete hai ki inhen sanbhaalane kii shakti bhi keval mahabali hanuman main hi thi
 - The most valuable things in the world are the nine funds which after getting them do not require any kind of wealth and property
 - isi prakaar asht siddhiyaan duniya kii sabase badi taaqat hai, jinhen paa lene ke baad vyakti sarv-shaktimaan ho jaataa he- ye nidhiyaan or siddhiyaan saamaanya dasha main nahin mil sakati- inhen paane ke liye bhagwaan kii vishesh krupa jaruri he- nidhiyon or siddhiyon paa lenaa hi badi baat nahin hoti, inhen apane paas rakh paanaa bhi behad mushkil hota he- jaraa si chook ho jane par ye nidhiyaan or siddhiyaan chhin bhi sakati hai- keval hanuman ji hi aise dev hai jo asht siddhiyon or nau nidhiyon se sampann hai- or hanuman ji kii puja upasna karne se ye siddhiyaan or nidhiyaan praapt bhi kii ja sakati hankeval hanuman ji kii hi krupa se vyakti ko ye aath siddhiyaan or nau nidhiyaan mil sakati hai lekin aashcharya kii baat ye ki mahabali hanuman kii bhakthi karne waalon ko naa hi kisi siddhi kii chaah hoti he, naa hi nidhi kii kaamana
 According to experts, if a person gets these attainments or funds, then he can achieve anything in the world
 siddhiyon or nidhiyon kii mahima ?- kul milakar prakaar aath siddhiyaan hai- anima, laghima, garima, prapti, prakamya, mahima, isheitv or vashitv- jo vasteen bahut durlabh hoti hai wo nidhiyaan kehalaati hai, inkaa ullekh brahmand puraana evam vaayu puraana main miltaa he- inamen se nau pramukh nidhiyaan hai

 dizin or bild qualitisbase pehle baat karenge is smartphone ke dizin or bild quality kii

 displeis smartphone kii disple brit or colorphul he

 ) bhartiya samvidhan or kanoonon kii roshni main 'hindu' shabd ke aashay or paribhaasha ke bare main centre sarkaar soochna ke adhikaar (artiai) ke tahat maangi gai jaankaree uplabdh nahin kara saki he
 Social worker Chandrashekhar Gaur, a resident of Neemuch in Madhya Pradesh, said on Sunday that he had filed an application under RTI asking what was the meaning and definition of the word 'hindu' as per Indian Constitution and laws
 unhone kaha, 'meri artiai arji par bharat sarkaar ke grih mantralay kii ore se 31 july ko bheje gaye jawaab main kaha gaya ki kendriya lok soochna adhikari (sipiio) ke paas apekshit soochna uplabdh nahin he
 In his RTI application, Gaur had also sought to know from the government on what grounds in the country a community is considered Hindu and Hindus are treated like a majority
 lekin in sawaalon par yahi jawaab doharaa diya gaya ki 'apekshit soochna sipiio ke paas uplabdh nahin he
 ' saamaajik kaaryakarta ne kaha, 'meri artiai arji par sarkaar kaa jawaab hairaan karne vaala he
 If the government does not know what is the meaning and definition of the word Hindu, then what are the laws like the Hindu Marriage Act? ' gaur ne kaha, 'sarkaar ko yah bhi bataanaa chahie ki vah alag-alag shaskeey form bharwate vakt nagarikon se unki majahabi pahchaan kyon puuchhati he or jansankhya ke aankade dharmik aadhaar par kyon jari kiye jate hai
 Comments mashhoor vichaarak keen govindacharya ne 'hindu' shabd ko lekar daayar artiai arji par sarkari jawaab ke bare main puche jane par kaha, 'hindustan main sarkaar kii avadharana varsh 1935 ke bharat shashan adhinium ke jariye saamne ai, jabaki hindutv kaa vishay hajaaron saal purana he
 Governments should do more to understand philosophy like Hindutva
 ' The former national general secretary of the BJP said in his familiar style, 'indian society is not governed only by the state
 yah samaaj rajasatta ke saath dharmasatta, samajasatta or alpasatta se bhi chalata he
 The state needs to be aware of this
 ' He said, 'on my RTI application sent by the Ministry of Home Affairs, Government of India on 31 July, it was stated that the requisite information is not available with the Central Public Information Officer (CPIO)
 ' gaur ne apane artiai aavedan main sarkaar se yah bhi jaananaa chaha tha ki desh main kin aadhaaron par kisi samudaay ko hindu mana jaataa he or hinduon ko bahusnkhyakon kii tarah dekha jaataa he
 But the answer was repeated on these questions that 'requisite information is not available with CPIO
 ' The social worker said, 'the government's response to my RTI application is shocking
 agar sarkaar ko yah pataa hi nahin he ki hindu shabd kaa aashay or paribhaasha kya he, to hindu vivaah adhinium sareekhe kanoon aakhir kis aadhaar par bana die gaye
 'gaur said,' The government should also explain why it asks citizens to identify their religious identity while filling different government forms and why the population figures are released on religious grounds

 Yuvraj could not even open the account, while Gambhir scored 24 runs off 42 balls with the help of five fours
 gambheer ko tradewell ne apni gend par ian bel ke haathon kaich karaayaa

 dhoni ne 23 gendon par do chauke lagaae

 bharat ne mohali main khele gaye chauthe mukaable main paanch wicket kii jeet ke saath yah shrunkhlaa 3-1 se apane naam kar lee thi
 The first match was played in Rajkot, which was won by the English team
 iske baad bharat ne kochi, ranchi or mohali main hetric lagaakar elister cook ko post kiya tha
 It was a historic moment for the HPCA Stadium, located at an altitude of 1500 meters above sea level, for the first time an international match was played on this picturesque ground
 isse pehle yah indian premier lig maichon kii mejabani kar chukaa he, lekin antarrashtriya patal par aane kaa ise pehali baar mauka mila he

 But today it is included in the record book as a new international cricket venue
